Commit: https://github.com/plone/plone.app.event/commit/c4969f321c9c054d2bc8261bf4f4e266dd2236dd

Optimize next occurrences list in event_summary
Show only upcoming occurrences in the for ``@@event_summary`` for events with
occurrences. On the last occurrence, only a link to all occurrences via
``@@event_listing`` is shown.

Files changed:
M CHANGES.rst
M plone/app/event/browser/event_summary.pt
M plone/app/event/browser/event_summary.py
M plone/app/event/tests/test_event_summary.py
M plone/app/event/tests/test_event_view.py
